  Blockchains controller (acceptance)
    âœ” retrieves list of available blockchains
    âœ” retrieves the total count of blockchains
    âœ” retrieves the information of a specific blockchain (71ms)
    âœ” generate a mapping of the available aliases for the chains

  PingController
    âœ” invokes GET /ping

  V1 controller (acceptance)
    1) invokes GET /v1/{appId} and successfully relays a request
    2) returns 404 when no app is found
    3) returns 404 when the specified blockchain is not found
    4) internally performs successful sync check/chain check
    5) fails on request with invalid authorization header
    6) fails on request with invalid origin
    7) fails on gigastake relay with invalid secret key
    8) fails on gigastake relay with invalid origin
    9) fails on gigastake relay with invalid user agent
    10) success relay with correct secret key, origin and userAgent security
    11) performs a failed request returning error
    12) returns error on chain check failure
    13) succesfully relays a loadbalancer application
    14) succesfully relays a loadbalancer application with log limits
    15) returns an error when load balancer relay body is not a JSON
    16) returns an error when application relay body is not a JSON
    17) returns error when no load balancer is found
    18) returns error on load balancer relay failure
    19) returns error when altruist returns non-json string as response
    20) redirects empty path with specific load balancer
    21) fails on invalid redirect load balancer
    22) Perfoms sticky requests on LBs that support it using rpcID
    23) Perfoms sticky requests on LBs that support it using prefix
    24) Fails sticky requests due to not being on whitelist
    25) Pass sticky requests due to being on whitelist
    26) Returns error on get request to app/lb
    27) relays a gigastaked lb
    Rate-limiting applications and loadbalancers
      28) logs a warning on request with rate-limited app
      29) logs a warning on lb relay request with rate-limited app
    Contract/method whitelisting
      30) fails on request with restricted contract whitelist (eth_call)
      31) success on request with restricted contract whitelist (eth_call)
      32) fails on request with restricted contract whitelist (eth_sendRawTransaction)
      33) success on request with restricted contract whitelist (unsupported method)
      34) success on request with restricted contract whitelist (eth_sendRawTransaction)
      35) fails on request with restricted contract whitelist (eth_getLogs)
      36) success on request with restricted contract whitelist (eth_getLogs)
      37) fails on request with restricted contract whitelist (eth_getCode, eth_getBalance, eth_getStorageAt, eth_getTransactionCount)
      38) success on request with restricted contract whitelist (eth_getCode, eth_getBalance, eth_getStorageAt, eth_getTransactionCount)
      39) fails on request with restricted contract whitelist (bundled transactions)
      40) success on request with restricted contract whitelist (bundled transactions)
      41) fails on request with restricted method whitelist
      42) success on request with restricted method whitelist
      43) success on request without restricted method whitelist
      44) success on request without restricted contracts whitelist
      45) fails on request with restricted blockchain whitelist
      46) success on request with restricted blockchain whitelist
      47) fails on request with blocked contract address
